payplanlink.AmountOverride,payplanlink.FKey,payplanlink.LinkType,payplanlink.SecDateTEntry,      payplan.PatNum,payplan.dynamicPayPlanTPOption,payplan.PayPlanNum,      prodlink.Fee,prodlink.Num,prodlink.ClinicNum,prodlink.ProvNum,prodlink.ProcStatus,prodlink.DiscountPlanAmt      FROM payplanlink     INNER JOIN payplan ON payplan.PayPlanNum = payplanlink.PayPlanNum      LEFT JOIN (      SSELECT procedurelog.PatNum,        (procedurelog.ProcFee*(procedurelog.UnitQty+procedurelog.BaseUnits)         +COALESCE(procAdj.AdjAmt,0)+COALESCE(procClaimProc.InsPay,0)         +COALESCE(procClaimProc.WriteOff,0)         +COALESCE(procSplit.SplitAmt,0)        ) Fee,         procedurelog.ProcNum Num,payplanlink.LinkType,payplanlink.PayPlanLinkNum,procedurelog.ClinicNum,procedurelog.ProvNum,        procedurelog.ProcStatus,procedurelog.DiscountPlanAmt       FROM payplanlink       INNER JOIN procedurelog ON procedurelog.ProcNum=payplanlink.FKey AND payplanlink.LinkType=2       LEFT JOIN (       SSELECT SUM(adjustment.AdjAmt) AdjAmt,adjustment.ProcNum,adjustment.PatNum,adjustment.ProvNum,adjustment.ClinicNum       FROM adjustment       WHERE adjustment.PatNum IN (61)       GROUP BY adjustment.ProcNum,adjustment.PatNum,adjustment.ProvNum,adjustment.ClinicNum      )procAdj ON procAdj.ProcNum=procedurelog.ProcNum       AND procAdj.PatNum=procedurelog.PatNum       AND procAdj.ProvNum=procedurelog.ProvNum       AND procAdj.ClinicNum=procedurelog.ClinicNum      LEFT JOIN (       SSELECT SUM(COALESCE((CASE WHEN claimproc.Status IN (         1,4,7        ) THEN claimproc.InsPayAmt         WHEN claimproc.InsEstTotalOverride!=-1 THEN claimproc.InsEstTotalOverride ELSE claimproc.InsPayEst END),0)*-1) InsPay       ,SUM(COALESCE((CASE WHEN claimproc.Status IN (         1,4,7        ) THEN claimproc.WriteOff         WHEN claimproc.WriteOffEstOverride!=-1 THEN claimproc.WriteOffEstOverride         WHEN claimproc.WriteOffEst!=-1 THEN claimproc.WriteOffEst ELSE 0 END),0)*-1) WriteOff       ,claimproc.ProcNum       FROM claimproc        WHERE claimproc.Status!=2       AND claimproc.PatNum IN (61)       GROUP BY claimproc.ProcNum      )procClaimProc ON procClaimProc.ProcNum=procedurelog.ProcNum       LEFT JOIN (       SSELECT SUM(paysplit.SplitAmt)*-1 SplitAmt,paysplit.ProcNum       FROM paysplit       WHERE paysplit.PayPlanNum=0       AND paysplit.PatNum IN (61)       GROUP BY paysplit.ProcNum      )procSplit ON procSplit.ProcNum=procedurelog.ProcNum      UNION ALL      SSELECT adjustment.PatNum,adjustment.AdjAmt + COALESCE(adjSplit.SplitAmt,0) Fee,adjustment.AdjNum Num,payplanlink.LinkType       ,payplanlink.PayPlanLinkNum,adjustment.ClinicNum,adjustment.ProvNum,'0','0'       FROM payplanlink        INNER JOIN adjustment ON adjustment.AdjNum=payplanlink.FKey         AND payplanlink.LinkType=1       LEFT JOIN (        SSELECT SUM(COALESCE(paysplit.SplitAmt,0))*-1 SplitAmt,paysplit.AdjNum        FROM paysplit        WHERE paysplit.PayPlanNum=0        AND paysplit.PatNum IN (61)        GROUP BY paysplit.AdjNum       )adjSplit ON adjSplit.AdjNum=adjustment.AdjNum     ) prodlink ON Charges_61_90,GREATEST(transSums.Charges_31_60,0) Charges_31_60,GREATEST(transSums.Charges_0_30,0) Charges_0_30,transSums.TotalCredits - LEAST(transSums.ChargesOver90,0) - LEAST(transSums.Charges_61_90,0) - LEAST(transSums.Charges_31_60,0) - LEAST(transSums.Charges_0_30,0) TotalCredits,transSums.BalTotal,transSums.InsWoEst,transSums.InsPayEst,transSums.PayPlanDue FROM (SSELECT p.Guarantor PatNum,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate < '2022-03-16' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) ChargesOver90,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate < '2022-04-15' AND trans.TranDate >= '2022-03-16' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_61_90,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate < '2022-05-15' AND trans.TranDate >= '2022-04-15' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_31_60,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate <= '2022-06-14' AND trans.TranDate >= '2022-05-15' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_0_30,-SUM(CASE WHEN trans.TranAmount < 0 AND NOT(trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate <= '2022-06-14' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) TotalCredits,SUM(CASE WHEN trans.TranAmount != 0 THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) BalTotal,SUM(trans.InsWoEst) InsWoEst,SUM(trans.InsPayEst) InsPayEst,SUM(trans.PayPlanAmount) PayPlanDue FROM (SSELECT (CASE WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum=0 THEN tranbyproc.TranType ELSE 'SumByProcAndDate' END) TranType,0 PriKey,tranbyproc.PatNum,(CASE WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum!=0 AND SUM(tranbyproc.TranAmount) < 0 THEN tranbyproc.AgedProcDate ELSE tranbyproc.TranDate END) TranDate,SUM(tranbyproc.TranAmount) TranAmount,SUM(tranbyproc.PayPlanAmount) PayPlanAmount,SUM(tranbyproc.InsWoEst) InsWoEst,SUM(tranbyproc.InsPayEst) InsPayEst FROM (SSELECT 'Proc' TranType,pl.ProcNum PriKey,pl.PatNum,pl.ProcDate TranDate,pl.ProcFee*(pl.UnitQty+pl.BaseUnits) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst,0 AgedProcNum,'0001-01-01' AgedProcDate FROM procedurelog pl WHERE pl.ProcStatus=2 AND pl.ProcFee != 0 AND pl.PatNum IN (31,32) UNION ALL SSELECT 'Claimproc' TranType,cp.ClaimProcNum PriKey,cp.PatNum,cp.DateCP TranDate,(CASE WHEN cp.Status != 0 THEN (CASE WHEN cp.PayPlanNum = 0 THEN -cp.InsPayAmt ELSE 0 END) - cp.WriteOff ELSE 0 END) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,(CASE WHEN cp.Status = 0 THEN cp.WriteOff ELSE 0 END) InsWoEst,(CASE WHEN cp.Status = 0 THEN cp.InsPayEst ELSE 0 END) InsPayEst,0 AgedProcNum,'0001-01-01' AgedProcDate FROM claimproc cp LEFT JOIN payplan pp ON cp.PayPlanNum=pp.PayPlanNum WHERE cp.Status IN (0,1,4,5,7) AND cp.PatNum IN (31,32) HAVING TranAmount != 0 OR InsWoEst != 0 OR InsPayEst != 0 UNION ALL SSELECT 0 AND a.PatNum IN (31,32) UNION ALL SSELECT 'PatPay' TranType,ps.SplitNum PriKey,ps.PatNum,ps.DatePay TranDate,-ps.SplitAmt TranAmount,(CASE WHEN ps.PayPlanNum != 0 AND COALESCE(pp.IsClosed,0)=0 THEN TranAmount,ppc.Principal+ppc.Interest PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst,0 AgedProcNum,'0001-01-01' AgedProcDate FROM payplancharge ppc INNER JOIN payplan pp ON ppc.PayPlanNum=pp.PayPlanNum WHERE THEN ppc.Guarantor ELSE ppc.PatNum end) IN (31,32) UNION ALL     SSELECT 'PayPlanLink' TranType,ppl.PayPlanLinkNum PriKey,prodlink.PatNum PatNum,DATE(ppl.SecDateTEntry) TranDate,     (CASE WHEN ppl     LEFT JOIN (      SSELECT procedurelog.PatNum,(procedurelog.ProcFee*(procedurelog.UnitQty+procedurelog.BaseUnits)        +COALESCE(procAdj.AdjAmt,0)+COALESCE(procClaimProc.InsPay,0) tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_31_60,ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits < tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 THEN tSums.Charges_0_30 WHEN tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 + tSums.Charges_0_30 <= tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 + tSums.Charges_0_30 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_0_30,ROUND(tSums.BalTotal,3) BalTotal,ROUND(tSums.InsWoEst,3) InsWoEst,ROUND(tSums.InsPayEst,3) InsPayEst,ROUND(tSums.PayPlanDue,3) PayPlanDue FROM (SELECT transSums.PatNum,GREATEST(transSums.ChargesOver90,0) ChargesOver90,GREATEST(transSums.Charges_61_90,0) Charges_61_90,GREATEST(transSums.Charges_31_60,0) Charges_31_60,GREATEST(transSums.Charges_0_30,0) Charges_0_30,transSums.TotalCredits - LEAST(transSums.ChargesOver90,0) - LEAST(transSums.Charges_61_90,0) - LEAST(transSums.Charges_31_60,0) - LEAST(transSums.Charges_0_30,0) TotalCredits,transSums.BalTotal,transSums.InsWoEst,transSums.InsPayEst,transSums.PayPlanDue FROM (SELECT p.Guarantor PatNum,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate < '2022-03-16' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) ChargesOver90,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate < '2022-04-15' AND trans.TranDate >= '2022-03-16' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_61_90,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate < '2022-05-15' AND trans.TranDate >= '2022-04-15' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_31_60,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate <= '2022-06-14' AND trans.TranDate >= '2022-05-15' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_0_30,-SUM(CASE WHEN trans.TranAmount < 0 AND NOT(trans.TranType IN ('WriteoffOrig','SumByProcAndDate')) AND trans.TranDate <= '2022-06-14' THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) TotalCredits,SUM(CASE WHEN trans.TranAmount != 0 THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) BalTotal,SUM(trans.InsWoEst) InsWoEst,SUM(trans.InsPayEst) InsPayEst,SUM(trans.PayPlanAmount) PayPlanDue FROM (SELECT (CASE WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum=0 THEN tranbyproc.TranType ELSE 'SumByProcAndDate' END) TranType,0 PriKey,tranbyproc.PatNum,(CASE WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum!=0 AND SUM(tranbyproc.TranAmount) < 0 THEN tranbyproc.AgedProcDate ELSE tranbyproc.TranDate END) TranDate,SUM(tranbyproc.TranAmount) TranAmount,SUM(tranbyproc.PayPlanAmount) PayPlanAmount,SUM(tranbyproc.InsWoEst) InsWoEst,SUM(tranbyproc.InsPayEst) InsPayEst FROM (SELECT 'Proc' TranType,pl.ProcNum PriKey,pl.PatNum,pl.ProcDate TranDate,pl.ProcFee*(pl.UnitQty+pl.BaseUnits) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst,0 AgedProcNum,'0001-01-01' AgedProcDate FROM procedurelog pl WHERE pl.ProcStatus=2 AND pl.ProcFee != 0 UNION ALL SELECT 'Claimproc' TranType,cp.ClaimProcNum PriKey,cp.PatNum,cp.DateCP TranDate,(CASE WHEN cp.Status != 0 THEN (CASE WHEN cp.PayPlanNum = 0 THEN -cp.InsPayAmt ELSE 0 END) - cp.WriteOff ELSE 0 END) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,(CASE WHEN cp.Status = 0 THEN cp.WriteOff ELSE 0 END) InsWoEst,(CASE WHEN cp.Status = 0 THEN cp.InsPayEst ELSE 0 END) InsPayEst,0 AgedProcNum,'0001-01-01' AgedProcDate FROM claimproc cp AgedProcNum,'0001-01-01' AgedProcDate FROM payplancharge ppc INNER JOIN payplan pp ON ppc.PayPlanNum=pp.PayPlanNum WHERE ppc.ChargeDate <= '2022-06-24' AND ppc.ChargeType=0 AND !pp.IsClosed AND ppc.Principal+ppc.Interest != 0 AND pp.PlanNum=0 UNION ALL SELECT 'PPCComplete' TranType,ppc.PayPlanChargeNum PriKey,(CASE WHEN ppc.ChargeType = 0 THEN ppc.Guarantor ELSE pp.PatNum END) PatNum,ppc.ChargeDate TranDate,(CASE WHEN ppc.ChargeType != 0 THEN -ppc.Principal WHEN pp.PlanNum=0 THEN ppc.Principal+ppc.Interest ELSE 0 END) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst,(CASE payplanlink ppl     LEFT JOIN (      SELECT procedurelog.PatNum,(procedurelog.ProcFee*(procedurelog.UnitQty+procedurelog.BaseUnits)        +COALESCE(procAdj.AdjAmt,0)+COALESCE(procClaimProc.InsPay,0) "SELECT commlog.DateTStamp, patient.PatNum, CONCAT (patient.FName, ' ', patient.LName) AS Patient, patient.SSN AS SSN, DATE (appointment.AptDateTime) AS Appt, securitylog.LogDateTime AS CDate, ( 		CASE  			WHEN ISNULL(apptfield.FieldName) 				THEN 'No Selection' 			ELSE 'Insurance Verification' 			END 		) AS ApptFieldN, ( 		CASE  			WHEN ISNULL(apptfield.ApptFieldNum) 				THEN 'No Selection' 			ELSE apptfield.FieldValue 			END 		) AS ApptFieldV, a.ProcCode, GROUP_CONCAT(DISTINCT carrier.CarrierName ORDER BY patplan.Ordinal SEPARATOR ', ') AS Carriers, IFNULL(GROUP_CONCAT(commlog.Note ORDER BY commlog.CommDateTime SEPARATOR ' | '), 'No commlog entry') AS Commlog, patient.Birthdate AS Birthday FROM patient INNER JOIN appointment 	ON patient.PatNum = appointment.PatNum 		AND appointment.AptDateTime BETWEEN @FromDate AND @ToDate + INTERVAL 1 DAY INNER JOIN securitylog 	ON securitylog.FKey = appointment.AptNum 		AND securitylog.PermType = 25 		AND securitylog.PatNum = appointment.PatNum LEFT JOIN apptfield 	ON appointment.AptNum = apptfield.AptNum 		AND apptfield.FieldName LIKE @AptFieldName LEFT JOIN commlog 	ON commlog.PatNum = appointment.PatNum 		AND DATE (commlog.CommDateTime) = DATE (securitylog.LogDateTime) LEFT JOIN patplan 	ON patplan.PatNum = patient.PatNum LEFT JOIN inssub 	ON inssub.InsSubNum = patplan.InsSubNum LEFT JOIN insplan 	ON inssub.PlanNum = insplan.PlanNum LEFT JOIN carrier 	ON insplan.CarrierNum = carrier.CarrierNum LEFT JOIN ( 	SELECT procedurelog.ProcNum, procedurelog.AptNum, GROUP_CONCAT(procedurecode.ProcCode) AS ProcCode 	FROM procedurelog 	INNER JOIN procedurecode 		ON procedurelog.CodeNum = procedurecode.CodeNum 	GROUP BY procedurelog.AptNum 	) A 	ON A.AptNum = appointment.AptNum WHERE ISNULL(apptfield.FieldValue) 	OR apptfield.FieldValue REGEXP @AptFieldValues GROUP BY appointment.AptNum, apptfield.ApptFieldNum, apptfield.FieldValue ORDER BY appointment.AptDateTime;"	1
"SELECT p.ProcNum, p.CodeNum, CASE WHEN p.AptNum = 0 THEN NULL ELSE p.AptNum END AS AptNum, p.PatNum, p.ProvNum, p.ProcFee, DATE_ADD(DATE(p.ProcDate), INTERVAL 8 HOUR) as ProcDate, p.ProcStatus, CASE WHEN DATE(p.DateTP) < '2000-01-01' THEN NULL ELSE CONCAT(CONVERT(DATE(p.DateTP),char),'||',CONVERT(p.PatNum,char)) END AS ExternalTreatmentPlanID, DATE_ADD(DATE(p.DateTP), INTERVAL 8 HOUR) AS DateTP, pat.ResponsParty, pat.FeeSched, CASE WHEN DATE(apt.SecDateEntry) < '2000-01-01' THEN CASE WHEN DATE(apt.DateTStamp) < '2000-01-01' THEN NULL ELSE apt.DateTStamp END ELSE DATE_ADD(DATE(apt.SecDateEntry), INTERVAL 8 HOUR) END AS AptSecDateEntry , CASE WHEN DATE(apt.AptDateTime) < '2000-01-01' THEN NULL ELSEapt.AptDateTimeEND AS AptDateTime , DATE_ADD(DATE(CASE WHEN DATE(p.SecDateEntry) < '2000-01-01' THEN CASE WHEN DATE(p.DateTP) < '2000-01-01' THEN CASE WHEN DATE(p.DateEntryC) < DATE(p.ProcDate) THEN p.DateEntryC ELSE CASE WHEN DATE(p.ProcDate) < '2000-01-01' THEN p.DateEntryC ELSE p.ProcDate END END ELSE p.DateTP END ELSE p.SecDateEntry END), INTERVAL 8 HOUR) AS ProcSecDateEntry , CASE WHEN p.ProcStatus = 2 THEN DATE(p.ProcDate) ELSE NULL END AS ProcedureCompletedAt, NULL AS ProcedureRejectedAt FROM procedurelog AS p LEFT JOIN patient AS pat ON p.PatNum = pat.PatNum LEFT JOIN appointment AS apt ON p.AptNum = apt.AptNum;"	1
"select insplan.plannum as insid,employernum as empid,carrier.carriername as carrier,groupnum as groupnum,groupname as groupplan,address as add1,city as city,state as st,zip as zip,phone as contact,(select empname from employer where insplan.employernum = employer.employernum) as employername,(select sum(monetaryamt) from benefit where benefittype in ('5') and monetaryamt > 0 and benefit.plannum = insplan.plannum) as benifitind,carrier.`carriernum` as insuranceid , carrier.`electid` as payerid, address2 as add2 , feesched.description as feesched, replace(insplan.plannote,' ',' ') as notes from insplan left join carrier on insplan.carriernum = carrier.carriernum left join feesched on insplan.feesched = feesched.feeschednum;"	1

"UPDATE rcm_patplan_tbv AS dest1, ( 	SELECT a.* 	FROM ( 	SELECT insverhist.fkey, insverhist.datelastverified AS dateverified, insverhist.VerifyUserNum 	FROM insverifyhist insverhist 	WHERE Verifytype = 2 	AND insverhist.datelastverified > DATE_SUB(CURDATE(), INTERVAL 2 WEEK) 	ORDER BY datelastverified DESC 	) a 	GROUP BY fkey 	) AS src1 SET dest1.verifyusernum = src1.verifyusernum, dest1.dateverified = src1.dateverified WHERE dest1.patplannum = src1.fkey 	AND src1.dateverified >= dest1.dateinserted 	AND dest1.dateinserted > DATE_SUB(CURDATE(), INTERVAL 2 WEEK);"	1

"SELECT convert(right(p.patnum, 10), CHAR) AS key_value, convert(crc32(concat_ws('', right(p.patnum, 10), fname, lname, salutation, address, address2, city, STATE, zip, hmphone, wkphone, CASE  					WHEN patstatus = 0 						THEN 'a' 					ELSE 'i' 					END, CASE  					WHEN gender = '0' 						THEN 'm' 					WHEN gender = '1' 						THEN 'f' 					WHEN gender = '2' 						THEN 'u' 					END, guarantor, birthdate, right(priprov, 10), right(secprov, 10), CASE  					WHEN prefercontactmethod <> 1 						THEN 'y' 					ELSE 'n' 					END, bal_0_30, bal_31_60, bal_61_90, balover90, insest, datefirstvisit, pl.last_date_seen, employernum, CASE  					WHEN patstatus = 0 						THEN 'a' 					ELSE 'i' 					END, email, wirelessphone, CASE  					WHEN amtplanned > 0 						AND sum(CASE  								WHEN patplan.ordinal = 1 									THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 								ELSE 0 								END) > 0.01 						THEN sum(CASE  									WHEN patplan.ordinal = 1 										THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 									ELSE 0 									END) 					ELSE 0 					END, CASE  					WHEN amtplanned > 0 						AND sum(CASE  								WHEN patplan.ordinal = 2 									THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 								ELSE 0 								END) > 0.01 						THEN sum(CASE  									WHEN patplan.ordinal = 2 										THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 									ELSE 0 									END) 					ELSE 0 					END, p.BalTotal)), CHAR) AS check_sum, right(p.patnum, 10) AS patient_id, fname AS first_name, lname AS last_name, salutation, address AS address_1, address2 AS address_2, city, STATE, zip AS zipcode, hmphone AS home_phone, wkphone AS work_phone, CASE  		WHEN patstatus = 0 			THEN 'a' 		ELSE 'i' 		END AS STATUS, CASE  		WHEN gender = '0' 			THEN 'm' 		WHEN gender = '1' 			THEN 'f' 		WHEN gender = '2' 			THEN 'u' 		END AS 'sex', guarantor AS responsible_party_id, birthdate AS birth_date, right(priprov, 10) preferred_dentist, right(secprov, 10) AS Preferred_hygienist, CASE  		WHEN prefercontactmethod <> 1 			THEN 'y' 		ELSE 'n' 		END AS 'receive_recalls', bal_0_30 AS current_bal, bal_31_60 AS thirty_day, bal_61_90 AS sixty_day, balover90 AS ninety_day, insest AS estimated_insurance, datefirstvisit AS first_visit_date, pl.last_date_seen AS last_date_seen, employernum AS prim_employer_id, CASE  		WHEN patstatus = 0 			THEN 'a' 		ELSE 'i' 		END AS patient_status, email AS email_address, wirelessphone AS cell_phone, CASE  		WHEN amtplanned > 0 			AND sum(CASE  					WHEN patplan.ordinal = 1 						THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 					ELSE 0 					END) > 0.01 			THEN sum(CASE  						WHEN patplan.ordinal = 1 							THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 						ELSE 0 						END) 		ELSE 0 		END prim_benefits_remaining, CASE  		WHEN amtplanned > 0 			AND sum(CASE  					WHEN patplan.ordinal = 2 						THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 					ELSE 0 					END) > 0.01 			THEN sum(CASE  						WHEN patplan.ordinal = 2 							THEN ifnull(annualmax.annualmax, 0) - ifnull(used.amtused, 0) 						ELSE 0 						END) 		ELSE 0 		END sec_benefits_remaining, p.BalTotal total_balance FROM patient p LEFT JOIN patplan 	ON p.patnum = patplan.patnum LEFT JOIN inssub 	ON inssub.inssubnum = patplan.inssubnum LEFT JOIN ( 	SELECT patnum, max(procdate) last_date_seen 	FROM procedurelog 	GROUP BY patnum 	) pl 	ON pl.patnum = p.patnum LEFT JOIN ( 	SELECT benefit.plannum, max(benefit.monetaryamt) AS annualmax 	FROM benefit 	LEFT JOIN covcat 		ON covcat.covcatnum = benefit.covcatnum 	WHERE benefit.benefittype = 5 /* limitation */ 		AND benefit.timeperiod = 2 /* calendar year */ 		AND ( 			covcat.ebenefitcat = 1 			OR isnull(covcat.ebenefitcat) 			) 		AND benefit.monetaryamt > 0 /* (-1) indicates empty */ 	GROUP BY benefit.plannum 	) annualmax 	ON annualmax.plannum = inssub.plannum LEFT JOIN ( 	SELECT procedurelog.patnum, sum(procedurelog.procfee) AS amtplanned 	FROM procedurelog 	INNER JOIN patient 		ON patient.patnum = procedurelog.patnum 			AND patient.patstatus = 0 /* patient */ 	LEFT JOIN appointment a 		ON procedurelog.patnum = a.patnum 			AND a.aptstatus = 1 /*sched*/ 	WHERE procedurelog.procstatus = 1 /*treatment planned*/ 		AND isnull(a.aptnum) 	GROUP BY patient.patnum 	) planned 	ON planned.patnum = p.patnum LEFT JOIN ( 	SELECT patplan.patplannum, sum(ifnull(claimproc.inspayamt, 0)) AS amtused 	FROM claimproc 	INNER JOIN inssub 		ON claimproc.inssubnum = inssub.inssubnum 	INNER JOIN patplan 		ON inssub.inssubnum = patplan.inssubnum 			AND patplan.patnum = claimproc.patnum 	WHERE claimproc.STATUS IN (1, 3, 4) 		AND year(claimproc.procdate) = year(curdate()) /*current calendar year*/ 	GROUP BY patplan.patplannum 	) used 	ON used.patplannum = patplan.patplannum GROUP BY p.patnum;"	1

LinkNum,procedurelog.ProcNum,procedurelog.ProcDate AgeDate  						FROM payplanlink 						INNER JOIN payplan ON payplanlink.PayPlanNum=payplan.PayPlanNum 						INNER JOIN procedurelog ON procedurelog.ProcNum=payplanlink.FKey 							AND payplanlink.LinkType=2 							AND !(payplan.dynamicPayPlanTPOption=1 AND procedurelog.ProcStatus!=2) 						LEFT JOIN ( 							SELECT SUM(adjustment.AdjAmt) AdjAmt,adjustment.ProcNum,adjustment.PatNum,adjustment.ProvNum,adjustment.ClinicNum 							FROM adjustment GROUP BY adjustment.ProcNum,adjustment.PatNum,adjustment.ProvNum,adjustment.ClinicNum 						)procAdj ON procAdj.ProcNum=procedurelog.ProcNum 							AND procAdj.PatNum=procedurelog.PatNum 							AND procAdj.ProvNum=procedurelog.ProvNum 							AND procAdj.ClinicNum=procedurelog.ClinicNum 						LEFT JOIN ( 							SELECT SUM(COALESCE((CASE WHEN claimproc.Status IN ( 								1,4,7 							) THEN claimproc.InsPayAmt  								WHEN claimproc.InsEstTotalOverride!=-1 THEN claimproc.InsEstTotalOverride ELSE claimproc.InsPayEst END),0)*-1) InsPay 							,SUM(COALESCE((CASE WHEN claimproc.Status IN ( 								1,4,7 							)	THEN claimproc.WriteOff  								WHEN claimproc.WriteOffEstOverride!=-1 THEN claimproc.WriteOffEstOverride  								WHEN claimproc.WriteOffEst!=-1 THEN claimproc.WriteOffEst ELSE 0 END),0)*-1) WriteOff 							,claimproc.ProcNum 							FROM claimproc  							WHERE claimproc.Status!=2 GROUP BY claimproc.ProcNum 						)procClaimProc ON procClaimProc.ProcNum=procedurelog.ProcNum  						LEFT JOIN ( 							SELECT SUM(paysplit.SplitAmt)*-1 SplitAmt,paysplit.ProcNum 							FROM paysplit 							WHERE paysplit.PayPlanNum=0 GROUP BY paysplit.ProcNum 						)procSplit ON procSplit.ProcNum=procedurelog.ProcNum 					UNION ALL  						SELECT adjustment.PatNum,adjustment.AdjAmt + COALESCE(adjSplit.SplitAmt,0) Fee,payplanlink.PayPlanLinkNum LinkNum 							,0 ProcNum,DATE('0001-01-01') AgeDate  						FROM payplanlink  						INNER JOIN adjustment ON adjustment.AdjNum=payplanlink.FKey  							AND payplanlink.LinkType=1  						LEFT JOIN ( 								SELECT SUM(COALESCE(paysplit.SplitAmt,0))*-1 SplitAmt,paysplit.AdjNum 								FROM paysplit 								WHERE paysplit.PayPlanNum=0 GROUP BY paysplit.AdjNum 						)adjSplit ON adjSplit.AdjNum=adjustment.AdjNum 					) prodlink ON prodlink.LinkNum=ppl.PayPlanLinkNum ) tranbyproc GROUP BY tranbyproc.PatNum,tranbyproc.AgedProcNum,tranbyproc.TranDate,(CASE WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum=0 THEN tranbyproc.TranType ELSE 'SumByProcAndDate' END),(CASE WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum=0 AND tranbyproc.TranAmount >= 0 THEN 'credit' WHEN tranbyproc.AgedProcNum=0 AND tranbyproc.TranAmount < 0 THEN 'charge' ELSE 'SumByProcAndDate' END)) trans INNER JOIN patient p ON p.PatNum=trans.PatNum GROUP BY p.Guarantor) transSums) tSums) guarAging INNER JOIN patient ON patient.PatNum=guarAging.PatNum WHERE (guarAging.BalOver90 >= 0.005 OR guarAging.Bal_61_90 >= 0.005 OR guarAging.Bal_31_60 >= 0.005 OR guarAging.Bal_0_30 >= 0.005) ORDER BY patient.LName,patient.FName"	0

"select * from ( SELECT guarAging.Patnum as guarid ,guarAging.Bal_0_30 as Amtless30,guarAging.Bal_31_60 as Amt30to60 ,guarAging.Bal_61_90 as Amt60to90 ,guarAging.BalOver90 as Amt90above ,guarAging.BalTotal as TotalAR,'' as curdate,'' as payplanamt, guarAging.practiceid as practiceid FROM (SELECT tSums.PatNum, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits >= tSums.ChargesOver90 THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) BalOver90, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits <= tSums.ChargesOver90 THEN tSums.Charges_61_90 WHEN tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 <= tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_61_90, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits < tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 THEN tSums.Charges_31_60 WHEN tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 <= tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_31_60, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits < tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 THEN tSums.Charges_0_30 WHEN tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 + tSums.Charges_0_30 <= tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 + tSums.Charges_0_30 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_0_30 ,ROUND(tSums.BalTotal,3) BalTotal, ROUND(tSums.InsWoEst,3) InsWoEst,ROUND(tSums.InsPayEst,3) InsPayEst,ROUND(tSums.PayPlanDue,3) PayPlanDue,tSums.practiceid FROM (SELECT p.Guarantor PatNum,SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND trans.TranDate < date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 90.0 DAY) THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) ChargesOver90, SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND trans.TranDate < date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 60.0 DAY) AND trans.TranDate >= date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 90.0 DAY) THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_61_90, SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND trans.TranDate < date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 30.0 DAY) AND trans.TranDate >= date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 60.0 DAY) THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_31_60 , SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND trans.TranDate <= CURRENT_DATE AND trans.TranDate >= date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 30.0 DAY) THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_0_30, -SUM(CASE WHEN trans.TranType != 'WriteoffOrig' AND trans.TranAmount < 0 AND trans.TranDate <= CURRENT_DATE THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) TotalCredits,SUM(CASE WHEN trans.TranAmount != 0 THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) BalTotal, SUM(trans.InsWoEst) InsWoEst,SUM(trans.InsPayEst) InsPayEst,SUM(trans.PayPlanAmount) PayPlanDue,p.clinicnum as practiceid FROM (SELECT 'Proc' TranType,pl.ProcNum PriKey,pl.PatNum,pl.ProcDate TranDate,pl.ProcFee*(pl.UnitQty+pl.BaseUnits) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst FROM procedurelog pl WHERE pl.ProcStatus=2 AND pl.ProcFee != 0 UNION ALL SELECT 'Claimproc' TranType,cp.ClaimProcNum PriKey,cp.PatNum,cp.DateCP TranDate,(CASE WHEN cp.Status != 0 THEN (CASE WHEN cp.PayPlanNum = 0 THEN -cp.InsPayAmt ELSE 0 END) - cp.WriteOff ELSE 0 END) TranAmount,(CASE WHEN cp.PayPlanNum != 0 AND cp.Status IN(1,4,5) AND COALESCE(pp.IsClosed,0)=0 THEN -cp.InsPayAmt ELSE 0 END) PayPlanAmount,(CASE WHEN cp.Status = 0 THEN cp.WriteOff ELSE 0 END) InsWoEst,(CASE WHEN cp.Status = 0 THEN cp.InsPayEst ELSE 0 END) InsPayEst FROM claimproc cp LEFT JOIN payplan pp ON cp.PayPlanNum=pp.PayPlanNum WHERE cp.status IN (0,1,4,5,7) HAVING TranAmount != 0 OR PayPlanAmount != 0 OR InsWoEst != 0 OR InsPayEst != 0 UNION ALL SELECT 'Adj' TranType,a.AdjNum PriKey,a.PatNum,a.AdjDate TranDate,a.AdjAmt TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst FROM adjustment a WHERE a.AdjAmt != 0 UNION ALL SELECT 'PatPay' TranType,ps.SplitNum PriKey,ps.PatNum,ps.DatePay TranDate,-ps.SplitAmt TranAmount,(CASE WHEN ps.PayPlanNum != 0 AND COALESCE(pp.IsClosed,0)=0 THEN -ps.SplitAmt ELSE 0 END) PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst FROM paysplit ps LEFT JOIN payplan pp ON ps.PayPlanNum=pp.PayPlanNum WHERE ps.SplitAmt != 0 UNION ALL SELECT 'PPCharge' TranType,ppc.PayPlanChargeNum PriKey,ppc.Guarantor PatNum,ppc.ChargeDate TranDate,0 TranAmount,(CASE WHEN COALESCE(pp.IsClosed,0)=0 THEN COALESCE(ppc.Principal+ppc.Interest,0) ELSE 0 END) PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst FROM payplancharge ppc LEFT JOIN payplan pp ON ppc.PayPlanNum=pp.PayPlanNum WHERE ppc.ChargeDate <= DATE_ADD(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 10.0 DAY) AND ppc.ChargeType=0 AND COALESCE(ppc.Principal+ppc.Interest,0) != 0 UNION ALL SELECT 'PPCComplete' TranType,ppc.PayPlanChargeNum PriKey,(CASE WHEN ppc.ChargeType = 0 THEN ppc.Guarantor ELSE pp.PatNum END) PatNum,ppc.ChargeDate TranDate,(CASE WHEN ppc.ChargeType != 0 THEN -ppc.Principal WHEN pp.PlanNum=0 THEN ppc.Principal+ppc.Interest ELSE 0 END) TranAmount,0 PayPlanAmount,0 InsWoEst,0 InsPayEst FROM payplancharge ppc LEFT JOIN payplan pp ON pp.PayPlanNum=ppc.PayPlanNum WHERE ppc.ChargeDate <= DATE_ADD(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 10.0 DAY) ) trans INNER JOIN patient p ON p.PatNum=trans.PatNum GROUP BY p.Guarantor ORDER BY NULL) tSums) guarAging ) a where (a.AmtLess30+a.Amt30to60+a.Amt60to90+a.Amt90Above)<>0;"	1

"select * from ( SELECT guarAging.Patnum as guarid ,guarAging.Bal_0_30 as Amtless30,guarAging.Bal_31_60 as Amt30to60 ,guarAging.Bal_61_90 as Amt60to90 ,guarAging.BalOver90 as Amt90above ,guarAging.BalTotal as TotalAR,'' as curdate,'' as payplanamt, guarAging.practiceid as practiceid FROM (SELECT tSums.PatNum, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits >= tSums.ChargesOver90 THEN 0 ELSE tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_61_90, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits < tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 THEN tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_31_60, ROUND(CASE WHEN tSums.TotalCredits < tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 THEN tSums.Charges_0_30 WHEN tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 + tSums.Charges_0_30 <= tSums.TotalCredits THEN 0 ELSE tSums.ChargesOver90 + tSums.Charges_61_90 + tSums.Charges_31_60 + tSums.Charges_0_30 - tSums.TotalCredits END,3) Bal_0_30 ,ROUND(tSums.BalTotal,3) BalTotal, ROUND(tSums.InsWoEst,3) InsWoEst,ROUND(tSums.InsPayEst,3) InsPayEst,ROUND(tSums.PayPlanDue,3) PayPlanDue,tSums.practiceid FROM ChargesOver90, SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND trans.TranDate < date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 60.0 DAY) AND trans.TranDate >= date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 90.0 DAY) THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_61_90, SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND trans.TranDate < date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 30.0 DAY) AND trans.TranDate >= date_sub(CURRENT_DATE, INTERVAL 60.0 DAY) THEN trans.TranAmount ELSE 0 END) Charges_31_60 , SUM(CASE WHEN (trans.TranAmount > 0 OR trans.TranType = 'WriteoffOrig') AND "SELECT p.PatNum 'PMPatientID', annualmax.AnnualMax - COALESCE(used.AmtUsed, 0) 'RemainingBen' FROM patient p INNER JOIN patplan  ON p.PatNum = patplan.PatNum INNER JOIN inssub  ON inssub.InsSubNum = patplan.InsSubNum INNER JOIN insplan ip  ON ip.PlanNum = inssub.PlanNum INNER JOIN (  SELECT benefit.PlanNum, MAX(benefit.MonetaryAmt) AS AnnualMax  FROM benefit  LEFT JOIN covcat   ON covcat.CovCatNum = benefit.CovCatNum  WHERE benefit.BenefitType = 5   AND benefit.TimePeriod = 2   AND (    covcat.EbenefitCat = 1    OR ISNULL(covcat.EbenefitCat)    )   AND benefit.MonetaryAmt > 0  GROUP BY benefit.PlanNum  ) annualmax  ON annualmax.PlanNum = inssub.PlanNum INNER JOIN (  SELECT patient.PatNum, SUM(pl.ProcFee) AS AmtPlanned  FROM patient  INNER JOIN (   SELECT PatNum, ProcFee   FROM procedurelog   WHERE ProcStatus = 1    AND ProcFee != 0   ) pl   ON patient.PatNum = pl.PatNum  WHERE patient.PatStatus = 0   AND patient.ClinicNum IN (0)  GROUP BY patient.PatNum  ) planned  ON planned.PatNum = p.PatNum   AND planned.AmtPlanned > 0 LEFT JOIN (  SELECT patplan.PatPlanNum, SUM(claimproc.InsPayAmt) AS AmtUsed  FROM claimproc  INNER JOIN inssub   ON claimproc.InsSubNum = inssub.InsSubNum  INNER JOIN patplan   ON inssub.InsSubNum = patplan.InsSubNum    AND patplan.PatNum = claimproc.PatNum  WHERE claimproc.STATUS IN (1, 3, 4)   AND claimproc.ClinicNum IN (0)   AND YEAR(claimproc.ProcDate) = YEAR(CURDATE())   AND claimproc.InsPayAmt != 0  GROUP BY patplan.PatPlanNum  ) used  ON used.PatPlanNum = patplan.PatPlanNum WHERE PatStatus = 0 AND p.ClinicNum IN (0);"	1

"select appt.aptnum AS 'id',     appt.aptstatus AS aptstatus, pat.patnum AS 'pat', Concat(pat.fname, ' ', pat.lname) AS 'fullname',     prov.abbr AS 'provider', provh.abbr AS 'hygienist',     pat.email, pat.hmphone AS hmphone, pat.wirelessphone AS cell,     CASE WHEN pat.premed = 0 THEN '' ELSE premed END AS 'premed', pat.discountplannum,     Date_format(appt.aptdatetime, '%h:%i %p ') AS 'apttime',     appt.aptdatetime AS 'aptdate',     CASE WHEN appt.isnewpatient = true THEN 'Yes' ELSE '' END AS 'newpatient', appt.procdescript, appt.note AS 'apptnote',     CASE WHEN nitrous.fieldvalue = 'Y' THEN 'Nitrous' ELSE '' END AS 'nitrous',     CASE WHEN sedative.fieldvalue = 'Y' THEN 'Sedative' ELSE '' END AS 'sedative',     NULL as npdate, NULL as hhdate, appt.confirmed, appt.op, date(pat.birthdate) as birthdate,     appt.clinicnum      FROM patient pat      INNER JOIN appointment appt     ON pat.patnum = appt.patnum     AND appt.aptstatus IN( 1, 2, 4 )      and appt.clinicNum = 2           and appt.aptdatetime >= DATE_SUB(curdate(), INTERVAL 5 DAY)   and appt.aptdatetime <= DATE_ADD(curdate(), INTERVAL 5 DAY)           INNER JOIN provider prov ON appt.provnum = prov.provnum     LEFT JOIN provider provh ON appt.provhyg = provh.provnum AND appt.ishygiene = 1      LEFT JOIN patfield nitrous ON pat.patnum = nitrous.patnum AND nitrous.fieldname = 'Nitrous'     LEFT JOIN patfield sedative ON pat.patnum = sedative.patnum AND sedative.fieldname = 'Sedative'      GROUP BY appt.patnum, appt.aptnum ORDER BY appt.aptdatetime;"	1

"select pp.patplannum as id, iplan.monthrenew, pp.patnum as pat, cp.plannum, c.carriername,      SUM(cp.inspayamt) as inspayments,     cp.dedapplied as deductapplied,     yearlymax.monetaryamt as anmax,     individdeduct.monetaryamt as deduct,     familydeduct.monetaryamt as famdeduct,     (individdeduct.monetaryamt - cp.dedapplied) as deductremain,     case when ROUND((yearlymax.monetaryamt - SUM(IFNULL(cp.inspayamt,0)) - IFNULL(refresh.inspayest,0)),2) <0 then 0     else ROUND((yearlymax.monetaryamt - SUM(IFNULL(cp.inspayamt,0)) - IFNULL(refresh.inspayest,0)),2) end as maxremaining,      refresh.refreshdate+interval 1 year as refreshdate      from patplan pp      inner join inssub isub on isub.inssubnum = pp.inssubnum     inner join insplan iplan on isub.plannum=iplan.plannum     inner join carrier c on c.carriernum = iplan.carriernum      inner join (     select DISTINCT insplan.plannum,     STR_TO_DATE(CONCAT(Case when monthrenew > MONTH(CURDATE()) then YEAR(CURDATE())-1 else YEAR(NOW()) END,'-', CASE when monthrenew=0 then 1 else monthrenew END,'-',01),'%Y-%m-%d') as refreshdate,     sum(cpest.inspayest) as inspayest      from insplan     inner join inssub on insplan.plannum=inssub.plannum     inner join patplan on inssub.inssubnum=patplan.inssubnum     and patplan.patnum='38567'      left join     (       select inspayest, plannum, patnum, procdate       from claimproc       where patnum='38567'       and status=0     )     cpest     on cpest.patnum=patplan.patnum     and insplan.plannum=cpest.plannum     and cpest.procdate >=STR_TO_DATE(CONCAT(Case when monthrenew > MONTH(CURDATE()) then YEAR(CURDATE())-1 else YEAR(NOW()) END,'-', CASE when monthrenew=0 then 1 else monthrenew END,'-',01),'%Y-%m-%d')     group by insplan.plannum     ) refresh on iplan.plannum=refresh.plannum      left join     (       select SUM(inspayamt) as inspayamt, sum(dedapplied) dedapplied, patnum, plannum, procdate       from claimproc       where patnum='38567'       group by plannum, procdate     )     cp     on cp.patnum=pp.patnum     and refresh.plannum=cp.plannum     and cp.procdate >=refresh.refreshdate      left join benefit yearlymax     on yearlymax.benefitType=5     and yearlymax.covcatnum=0     and iplan.plannum=yearlymax.plannum     and coveragelevel=1     and yearlymax.codenum=0      left join benefit individdeduct     on individdeduct.benefitType=2     and individdeduct.covcatnum=0     and individdeduct.coveragelevel=1     and iplan.plannum=individdeduct.plannum     and individdeduct.codenum=0      left join benefit familydeduct     on familydeduct.benefitType=2     and familydeduct.covcatnum=0     and familydeduct.coveragelevel=2     and iplan.plannum=familydeduct.plannum     where pp.patnum='38567'     group by pp.patnum, iplan.plannum;"	1
